  *Intro - Rhy. Fig. 1*  
  *Verse 1 - w/ Rhy. Fig. 1*  
  Hey mister, where you headed?

  I need a lift to happy hour.  
  Say oh no.  
  Do you brake for distilled spirits?  
  I need a break as well.  
  The well that inebriates the guilt.  
  1, 2. 1, 2, 3, 4.

  *Here's how it goes, with the lyrics:*  
  *Do Verse part.*  
  I declare I don't care no more,  
  burning up and out and going bored,  
  in my smoked out boring room,  
  my hair is shagging in my eyes,  
  dragging my feet to hit the street tonight,  
  to drive along thse shit-town lights,  
  *Do Chorus Part:*  
  I'm not growing up,  
  I'm just Burning out,  
  and I stepped in line to walk amongst the dead,  
  *Do verse part:*  
  Apathy has rained on me,  
  and now I'm feeling like a soggy dream,  
  so close to drowning but I don't mind,  
  I've lived inside this Mental cave,  
  throw my emotions in the grave,  
  hell, who needs them anyway,  
  *Do Chorus*  
  *(When BJ says "Dead...." a secong time, do a [x577xx] and then it goes*  
  *into Bridge)*  
  *Do Bridge*

  *(BJ once again does the "dead...." thing, so do a [x577xx] 'till it goes*  
  *into the End-Bridge)*  
  *Do End-Bridge*  
  I am SO good!

  *some luck,*  
  *this song will show up on Green Day's new album, along with "Geek Stink Love",*

  *Verse 1 w/ Verse Riff*  
  I've got some scattered pictures lying on my bedroom floor.  
  Reminds me of the times we shared.  
  Makes me wish that you were here.  
  Now it seems I've forgotten my purpose in this life.  
  All the songs have been erased.  
  Guess I've learned from my mistakes.  
  *Chorus w/ Chorus Riff*  
  Open the past and present.  
  Now and we are there.  
  Story to tell and I am listening.  
  Open the bast and present.  
  And the future too.  
  It's all I've got and I'm giving it up to you.  
  *Verse 2 w/ Verse Riff*  
  Loose ends tied in knots.  
  Leaving a lump down in my throat.  
  Gagging on a souvenir.  
  Lodged to fill another year.  
  Drag it on and on until my skin is ripped to shreds.  
  Leaving my self wide open.  
  Living out a sacrifice.

  If you got no one and I've got no place to go, would it be alright?

  *TAB Notation:*  
  *Throughout this guide, you may find various symbols coinsiding with the*  
  *numbers of the TAB. This is a small legend letting you know what they mean.*  
  *If you are unfamiliar with how to accomplish the effects with the given*  
  *notation, I suggest you look on the web, there's plenty of info somewhere*  
  *out there on how to make all of these work to your full benefit.*  
  *h  = hammer-on*  
  *p  = pull-off*  
  *b  = bend*  
  *r  = bend release*

  *notation, I suggest you look on the web, there's plenty of info somewhere*

Nimrod (1997)  
  King For A Day  
  
  *TAB Notation:*  
  *Throughout this guide, you may find various symbols coinsiding with the*  
  *numbers of the TAB. This is a small legend letting you know what they mean.*  
  *If you are unfamiliar with how to accomplish the effects with the given*  
  *notation, I suggest you look on the web, there's plenty of info somewhere*  
  *out there on how to make all of these work to your full benefit.*  
  *h  = hammer-on*  
  *p  = pull-off*  
  *b  = bend*  
  *r  = bend release*  
  */  = slide up/down*  
  *= natural harmonic*  
  *{5} = artifical harmonic*  
  *~  = vibrato*  
  *tr = trill*  
  
  *As much as I would have loved to include a full transcription of the brass*  
  *parts. My it's been months since I've played trumpet and my trumpet-guitar*  
  *transcribing abilities are limited, soo.. enjoy another "4 chord wonder" by*  
  *Green Day.*

  E|-2-----2---------|-2-----2---------|-3---------------|-6---------------|]  
  
  *Okay, this song is very cool. These are the main riffs. There are plenty of*  
  *sites out there where you can listen to a RealAudio of the song, which is*  
  *what I transcribed it from, otherwise if you have the Hitchin' single, hell,*  
  *you're laughing. Thanks to Franklin Suco for suggesting this song to me and*  
  *sending me his original transcription of it. Although lacking a bassline and*  
  *some of the notes in the main Guitar Riff it was a great starter, thanks*  
  *dude. Enjoy!*

     'stoned....................'

  *notation, I suggest you look on the web, there's plenty of info somewhere*

  *end ***on A5***

Nimrod (1997)  
  Platypus (I Hate You)  
  
  *TAB Notation:*  
  *Throughout this guide, you may find various symbols coinsiding with the*  
  *numbers of the TAB. This is a small legend letting you know what they mean.*

  *WARNING!!!: If played properly, this song can really hurt your wrist,elbow,*  
  *shoulder and hand. This song makes Basket Case seem like a slow waltz.*  
  *I minimally censored some of the lyrics,*  
  *even though we all know what they are.*  
  
  *Standard tuning*  
  
  *Chords:*  
  ***B***:  [7-9-9-*-*-*]     ***G***:  [3-5-5-*-*-*]*  
  ***F#***: [2-4-4-*-*-*]     ***A***:  [5-7-7-*-*-*]*  
  ***E***:  [*-7-9-9-*-*]     ***A#***: [6-8-8-*-*-*]*

  *Almost the entire song is played with up and*  
  *down super-strumming, unless otherwise noted*

  *Verse 1 w/ Verse Riff*  
  Another sentimental argument, and bitter love.  
  Fucked without a kiss again and dragged it through the mud.  
  Yelling at brick walls and punching windows made of stone.  
  The worry rock has turned to dust, and fallen on our pride.  
  A knocked down dragged out fight.  
  Fat lips and open wounds.  
  Another wasted night, and no one will take the fall.  
  Where do we go from where?  
  and what did you do with the directions?  
  Promise me no dead end streets and I'll guarantee we'll have the road.

  *TAB Notation:*  
  *Throughout this guide, you may find various symbols coinsiding with the*  
  *numbers of the TAB. This is a small legend letting you know what they mean.*  
  *If you are unfamiliar with how to accomplish the effects with the given*  
  *notation, I suggest you look on the web, there's plenty of info somewhere*  
  *out there on how to make all of these work to your full benefit.*  
  *h  = hammer-on*  
  *p  = pull-off*  
  *b  = bend*  
  *r  = bend release*  
  */  = slide up/down*  
  *= natural harmonic*  
  *{5} = artifical harmonic*  
  *~  = vibrato*  
  *tr = trill*

  *Here is a great green day song that I decided to fix up,*  
  *seeing that some of the other tabs arenXt completely*  
  *right. Billie uses a four string barre for open A's.*  
  *The e string is muffled. It's easier to do the intro this*  
  *way it is also easier to go to and from other barre chords.*

  *Throughout this guide, you may find various symbols coinsiding with the*  
  *numbers of the TAB. This is a small legend letting you know what they mean.*  
  *If you are unfamiliar with how to accomplish the effects with the given*  
  *notation, I suggest you look on the web, there's plenty of info somewhere*  
  *out there on how to make all of these work to your full benefit.*

  *numbers of the TAB. This is a small legend letting you know what they mean.*  
  *If you are unfamiliar with how to accomplish the effects with the given*  
  *notation, I suggest you look on the web, there's plenty of info somewhere*  
  *out there on how to make all of these work to your full benefit.*

  *Verse 1 w/ Verse Riff*  
  Haushinka is a girl with a peculiar name.  
  I met her on the eve of my birthday.  
  Did she know.  
  Did she know, before she went away.  
  Does she know?  
  But it's too damn late.  
  *Chorus w/ Chorus Riff*  
  This girl has gone far away.  
  Now she's gone.

  All I have now is a memory to date.  
  A cheap hat and cigarettes, and a peculiar name.  
  I didn't know.  
  I didn't know, before she went away.  
  I know now.  
  I know now, and it's too damn late.
